msg:The hotel is a five-star hotel with an excellent location. The lobby is spacious and has ground and underground parking lots. The surrounding area is a business district, and there is a Sinopec gas station next to it.
Booked a business standard room, the room facilities are simple and clean, the bathroom is separated from the room by floor-to-ceiling glass, the overall transparent and comfortable, equipped with a shower and bathtub, washing liquid, and all kinds of supplies.
According to our request, we sent a low pillow made of wheat skin, and also sent 2 bottles of drinking water. The floor attendant was very proactive. When he saw that we washed clothes, he sent hangers and laundry soap; when he saw that there was a computer on the desk, there was a steam hot compress eye mask on the bedside table, etc.... All this was very warm and made us feel at home.
The breakfast was very rich, with a reasonable combination of Chinese and Western food, and a special coffee machine. I have stayed in the hotel for 3 days, and the breakfast is changing every day, and I eat different food, which is great.

msg:There are several problems with this hotel:
1. The hotel said it was newly renovated, but the facilities inside were relatively old and the faucets in the bathroom were loose.
2. The sound insulation of the hotel is very poor. People nearby are talking and the roar of cars outside is endless. I originally thought we had opened the window ourselves, but after closing the window, the sound insulation was still not good.
3. Hotel rooms smell from each other, and the smell from the room to the corridor is very strong. Someone in the next room ate leeks, and the smell of leeks came to our room. Then someone might be smoking in the hallway, maybe in the next room, and then our whole room would smell like smoke. If you are sensitive to the smell of smoke, you should definitely not stay in this hotel.
4. What is particularly ironic is that the room states that smoking is not allowed, but there is an ashtray. I really donâ€™t know whether the hotel allows smoking or not. We have no objection to hotels letting people smoke, but it deprives us non-smokers of their rights. If a hotel states in advance that it is a hotel that allows smoking, it should make it clear in advance, so that non-smokers can make their own choices.
5. There is no small refrigerator in the room. At our request, one was temporarily moved from another room.
6. The service of the hotel waiters is quite enthusiastic, this cannot be denied. The location of the hotel is also good. It is located in the city center and is convenient to go everywhere. But overall, this hotel has a lot of room for improvement. In the current situation, we do not recommend it.
